       <script>
        function openNavigationLink(link) {
            var target = $(link).attr('data-target');
            var href = $(link).attr('href');

            if (target == 1) {
                window.open(href, "_blank");
            } else if (target == 2) {
                window.open(href, 'name', 'menubar=no,location=no,scrollbars=yes,status=no,toolbar=no,resizable=yes');
            } else {
                window.open(href, '_self');
            }
        }
       </script>

                    });
                      $('.triple-banner-js').slick({
                        slidesToShow: 1,
                        slidesToScroll: 1,
                        
                        arrows: true,
                        dots: false,
                        autoplay: false,
                        speed: 500,
                        infinite: true,
                        prevArrow: '<i class="thm-arrow2-left"></i>',

                    $('.double-banner-js').slick({
                        slidesToShow: 1,
                        slidesToScroll: 1,
                        
                        arrows: true,
                        dots: false,
                        autoplay: false,
                        speed: 500,
                        infinite: true,

                        nextArrow: '<i class="thm-arrow1-right2"></i>',
                        responsive:[
                             {
                            breakpoint: 3000,
                            settings:"unslick"
                          }, 
                            
                           {
                               breakpoint: 1025,
                                slidesToShow: 1,
                                slidesToScroll: 1,
                                settings:"slick"
                              } 
                         
                        ]
                    });
                    $('#home-banner-carousel-js').slick({
                        slidesToShow: 5,
                        slidesToScroll: 1,
                        asNavFor: '#home-banner-web-js',
                        dots: false,
                        focusOnSelect: true,
                        centerMode: true,
                        arrows:false
                    });
                });
                newHomepageSliderControl();

                function newHomepageSliderControl() {
                    $(document).ready(function () {
                        $('#home-banner-web-js').on('beforeChange', function(event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide){
                            $('#home-banner-carousel-js li:eq('+currentSlide+')').removeClass('slick-current');
                            $('#home-banner-carousel-js li:eq('+nextSlide+')').addClass('slick-current');
                        });

                        var percentTime;
                        var tick;
                        var time = 1;
                        var progressBarIndex = 0;
                        var isPause;

                        $('#home-banner-web-js, #home-banner-carousel-js').on({
                            mouseenter: function() {
                                isPause = true;
                            },
                            mouseleave: function() {
                                isPause = false;
                            },
                            blur: function() {
                                isPause = false;
                            }
                        });

                        function startProgressbar() {
                            resetProgressbar();
                            percentTime = 0;
                            isPause = false;
                            tick = setInterval(interval, 8);
                        }

                        function interval() {
                            if (isPause === false) {
                                percentTime += 1 / (time + 5);
                                $('#in-progress-' + progressBarIndex + '-js').css({
                                    width: percentTime + "%"
                                });
                                if (percentTime >= 100) {
                                    $('#home-banner-web-js').slick('slickNext');
                                    progressBarIndex++;
                                    if (progressBarIndex > 4) {
                                        progressBarIndex = 0;
                                    }
                                    startProgressbar();
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        function resetProgressbar() {
                            $('.inProgress-js').css({
                                width: 0 + "%"
                            });
                            clearInterval(tick);
                        }
                        startProgressbar();

                        $('#home-banner-carousel-js li').click(function () {
                            clearInterval(tick);
                            var goToThisIndex = $(this).data("slickIndex");
                            progressBarIndex = goToThisIndex;
                            $('#home-banner-carousel-js').slick('slickGoTo', goToThisIndex, false);
                            startProgressbar();
                        });

                        $('#home-banner-web-js, #home-banner-carousel-js').on({
                            mouseover: function () {
                                $('#home-banner-web-js .thm-arrow2-left').css('visibility', 'visible');
                                $("#home-banner-web-js .thm-arrow1-right2").css('visibility', 'visible');
                            },
                            mouseout: function () {
                                $("#home-banner-web-js .thm-arrow2-left").css('visibility', 'hidden');
                                $("#home-banner-web-js .thm-arrow1-right2").css('visibility', 'hidden');
                            }
                        });

                        $('#home-banner-web-js .thm-arrow2-left').on('mousedown', function(e) {
                            clearInterval(tick);
                            var goToThisIndex = $('#home-banner-carousel-js .slick-current').data('slickIndex') - 1;
                            if(goToThisIndex == -1) {
                                goToThisIndex = 4;
                            }
                            console.log(goToThisIndex)
                            progressBarIndex = goToThisIndex;
                            $('#home-banner-carousel-js').slick('slickGoTo', goToThisIndex, false);
                            $('#home-banner-web-js').slick('slickPrev');
                            startProgressbar();
                        });

                        $('#home-banner-web-js .thm-arrow1-right2').on('mousedown', function() {
                            clearInterval(tick);
                            var goToThisIndex = $('#home-banner-carousel-js .slick-current').data('slickIndex') + 1;
                            if(goToThisIndex == 5) {
                                goToThisIndex = 0;
                            }
                            progressBarIndex = goToThisIndex;
                            $('#home-banner-carousel-js').slick('slickGoTo', goToThisIndex, false);
                            $('#home-banner-web-js').slick('slickNext');
                            startProgressbar();
                        });

                        $('#home-banner-web-js .thm-arrow2-left, #home-banner-web-js .thm-arrow1-right2').on('dblclick', function() {
                            clearInterval(tick);
                            var goToThisIndex = $('#home-banner-web-js .slick-current').data('slickIndex');
                            progressBarIndex = goToThisIndex;
                            $('#home-banner-carousel-js').slick('slickGoTo', goToThisIndex, false);
                            startProgressbar();
                        });

                        $('#home-banner-mobile-js').slick({
                                  dots: true,
                                  infinite: true,
                                  speed: 300,
                                  slidesToShow: 1,
                                  slidesToScroll: 1,
                                  autoplay: true,
                                  responsive: [
                                      {
                                          breakpoint: 1024,
                                          settings: {
                                              slidesToShow: 1,
                                              slidesToScroll: 1,
                                              infinite: true,
                                              dots: true
                                          }
                                      },
                                      {
                                          breakpoint: 600,
                                          settings: {
                                              slidesToShow: 1,
                                              slidesToScroll: 1
                                          }
                                      },
                                      {
                                          breakpoint: 480,
                                          settings: {
                                              slidesToShow: 1,
                                              slidesToScroll: 1
                                          }
                                      }
                                  ]
                              });
                              $('#home-banner-mobile-js').css('opacity', '1');

                    });
                }
  </script>

   <script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
            //email submit
            $(document).on('submit', '#email-subscribe-form-footer', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
//                console.log('email :::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::');
                var email = $('#footer_email').val().trim();
                var errorElement = $('#footer-email-error-element');
                if (email != '') {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        url: "//www.tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=newsletter&op=subscription&act=ajax_subscribe&ajax=true",
                        dataType: "json",
                        data: {
                            'email': email
                        },
                        success: function (data) {
                            if(data.statusCode && data.statusCode == 200){
                                $(errorElement).removeClass('error').addClass('success');
                            }else{
                                $(errorElement).removeClass('success').addClass('error');
                            }
                            errorElement.html(data.messages);
                            // console.info(':::::::::', data);
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
            //telephone submit
            $(document).on('submit', '#telephone-subscribe-form-footer', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
//                console.log('telephone :::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::');
                var element = $('#footer_telephone').val().trim();
                var errorElement = $('#footer-telephone-error-element');
                if (element != '') {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        url: "//www.tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=newsletter&op=sms_subscription&act=ajax_subscribe&ajax=true",
                        dataType: "json",
                        data: {
                            'telephone': element
                        },
                        success: function (data) {
                            if(data.statusCode && data.statusCode == 200){
                                $(errorElement).removeClass('error').addClass('success');
                            }else{
                                $(errorElement).removeClass('success').addClass('error');
                            }
                            errorElement.html(data.messages);
                            // console.info(':::::::::', data);
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
            $('#email-subscribe-form-footer').formValidator({
                errorsArray: '[{"value":"* ovo je obavezno polje!","error_code":0},{"value":"* unos je prekratak!","error_code":1},{"value":"* unos je preduga\u010dak!","error_code":2},{"value":"* samo slova!","error_code":3},{"value":"* samo brojevi!","error_code":4},{"value":"* samo brojevi, slova i crte!","error_code":5},{"value":"* e-mail adresa nije validna!","error_code":6},{"value":"* samo slova, razmaci i crte!","error_code":7},{"value":"* samo brojevi, slova i razmaci!","error_code":8}]',
                ccpid: '3',
                userTypeClassSelector: ''
            });
            $('#telephone-subscribe-form-footer').formValidator({
                errorsArray: '[{"value":"* ovo je obavezno polje!","error_code":0},{"value":"* unos je prekratak!","error_code":1},{"value":"* unos je preduga\u010dak!","error_code":2},{"value":"* samo slova!","error_code":3},{"value":"* samo brojevi!","error_code":4},{"value":"* samo brojevi, slova i crte!","error_code":5},{"value":"* e-mail adresa nije validna!","error_code":6},{"value":"* samo slova, razmaci i crte!","error_code":7},{"value":"* samo brojevi, slova i razmaci!","error_code":8}]',

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function () {

            //sendinBlueAPI
            $('.fnc-add-to-basket').sendinBlueAPI({
                trackEvent: true,
                trackType: 'add-to-basket'
            });

            $('.fnc-delete-basket-item').sendinBlueAPI({
                trackEvent: true,
                trackType: 'delete-from-basket'
            });

            $(document).sendinBlueAPI({
                identifyEmail: true,
                email: USER_EMAIL
            });


        // adding scroll in header basket in case there are more then 3 items in it
        $('.js-header-basket-product').css('max-height', '300px').mCustomScrollbar({
            theme: "dark-thin",
            mouseWheel: { scrollAmount: 240 }
        });
        // adding sroll in filters
        $('.js-filter-content').css('max-height', '260px').mCustomScrollbar({
            theme: "dark-thin",
            mouseWheel: { scrollAmount: 240 }
        });
        // Adding product to basket
        $('.fnc-add-to-basket').click(function () {
            var element = $(this);
            var url = $(this).attr("href");

            if (typeof url !== 'undefined') {
                if (element.hasClass('not-selling-on-webshop')) {
                    window.location.href = url;
                } else {
                    $.ajax({
                        url: url,
                        type: 'post',
                        dataType: "json",
                        success: function (data) {
                            if (data['sp_product_not_valid']) {
                                alert(data['sp_product_not_valid']);
                            } else if (typeof data['outlet'] !== 'undefined') {
                                alert(data['outlet']);
                            } else {
                                // Animation for adding product to basket
                                addToBasketAnimation(element, data);
                                $('.js-basket-icon').addClass('thm-cart-fill');
                                $('.js-basket-icon').removeClass('thm-cart-line');
                                if ($('.js-basket-header').children('span').hasClass('js-br-proizvoda') && typeof data['outlet'] == 'undefined') {
                                    $('.js-br-proizvoda').html(data['product_num']);
                                } else if (typeof data['outlet'] == 'undefined') {
                                    $('.js-basket-header a').prepend('<span class="js-br-proizvoda br-proizvoda"></span>');
                                    $('.js-br-proizvoda').html(data['product_num']);
                                }
                                           $('.js-br-proizvoda').addClass('br-proizvoda-big');
                                    $('.js-br-proizvoda').delay(400).queue(function(){
                                        $(this).removeClass('br-proizvoda-big').clearQueue() 
                            });
                            }
                        },
                        error: function (data) {
                            console.log(data);
                        }
                                   
                    });
                }
            }

            return false;
        });
        //floater banner
        $('#floater-banner-x').on('click', function() {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "//www.tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=banners&op=banners_ajax_control&type=floater_banner",
                success: function (data) {
                    $('#floater-banner-x').hide();
                    $('#floater-banner').hide();
                }
            });
        });
    });
    /**
     * Delete checkout item by it's id
     */
    $('.fnc-delete-basket-item').live('click', function () {
        var page_id = "home";

        if (page_id == 'one_page_checkout') {
            var basket_item_id = $(this).data('basket-item-id');
            var inst = $('[data-remodal-id=modal]').remodal();
            inst.open();
            $(document).on('confirmation', '.remodal', function () {
                $('[data-delete-basket-item=' + basket_item_id + ']').remove();
                $.ajax({
                    url: "//www.tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=catalog&op=one_page_checkout&act=ajax_checkout_delete_item",
                    type: 'post',
                    dataType: 'json',
                    data: {
                        "basket_item_id": basket_item_id
                    },
                    success: function (data) {
                        if (data['product_num'] == 0) {
                            $('.js-basket-product-num').remove();
                            window.location.replace('https://www.tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=catalog&op=basket');
                        } else {
                            var total_price = data['basket_items'].total_cena_niza_redovna.toLocaleString(
                                    'de-DE',
                                    {
                                        style: 'currency',
                                        currency: CURRENCY,
                                        minimumFractionDigits: 0
                                    }
                            );
                            var label_total_price = labels['for_payment'] + ' ';
                            $('.js-br-proizvoda').html(data['product_num']);
                            $('.js-basket-items-total-price').html(label_total_price + total_price);
                            $('.js-header-basket-total').html(total_price);
                            updatePrices(); // Update total prices
                        }
                    }
                });
            });
        } else {
            var basket_item_id = $(this).data('basket-item-id');
            $('[data-delete-basket-item=' + basket_item_id + ']').remove();
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "https://www.tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=catalog&op=basket&act=drop&ajax=1",
                dataType: "json",
                data: {
                    'basket_item_id': basket_item_id
                },
                success: function (data) {
                    if (data['product_num'] == 0) {
                        $('.js-basket-product-num').remove();                        
                        $('.js-basket-header i').addClass('thm-cart-line');
                        $('.js-basket-header i').removeClass('thm-cart-fill');
                        $('.header-basket-content-js').remove();
                        var total_price = data['basket_items'].total_cena_niza_redovna.toLocaleString(
                                    'de-DE',
                                    {
                                        style: 'currency',
                                        currency: CURRENCY,
                                        minimumFractionDigits: 0
                                    }
                            );
                    $('.js-header-basket-total').html(total_price);
                    } else {
                        if ($('.js-basket-items-total-price').length) {
                            var label_total_price = labels['for_payment'] + ' ';
                            var total_price = data['basket_items'].total_cena_niza_redovna.toLocaleString(
                                    'de-DE',
                                    {
                                        style: 'currency',
                                        currency: CURRENCY,
                                        minimumFractionDigits: 0
                                    }
                            );
                            $('.js-br-proizvoda').html(data['product_num']);
                            $('.js-basket-items-total-price').html(label_total_price + total_price);
                            $('.js-header-basket-total').html(total_price);
                        }
                    }
                },
                error: function (data) {
                    console.log(data);
                }
            });
        }
    });
  </script>

   $(document).ready(function () {
        var browserWidth = window.innerWidth;
        var imgsrc='';
        if(browserWidth> 1024) {
            imgsrc = $('.fnc-banner-image').data('image');
        } else {
            imgsrc = $('.fnc-banner-image').data('image-mobile');
        }
        $('.fnc-banner-image').attr('src', imgsrc);
    });
    $(window).resize(function () { 
        var browserWidth = window.innerWidth;
        var imgsrc='';
        if(browserWidth> 1024) {
            imgsrc = $('.fnc-banner-image').data('image');
        } else {
            imgsrc = $('.fnc-banner-image').data('image-mobile');
        }
        $('.fnc-banner-image').attr('src', imgsrc);
    });
  </script>

        function categoryMenu(){
            var browserWidth = window.innerWidth;
            //console.log('function categoryMenu bira da li ce da ide na categoryWeb ili categoryMob');
         
            //funkcija koja bira da li se ucitava web ili mobile meni
            if(browserWidth>1024){
                $("body").addClass('web');
                $("body").removeClass('mob');
                categoryWeb();
            }else if(browserWidth<1025){
                $("body").addClass('mob');
                $("body").removeClass('web');
            
                categoryMobile();               
            }                
        }
        
        function categoryMobile() {
            $('.user-wraper').click(function(e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                $(this).children('.dropdown-login').toggle();
            });
            $('.user-wraper input').click(function(e){
                e.stopPropagation();
            });
            console.log('function categoryMob');
             $('.header-fixed-wrap').css({'height':'125px','margin-top':'0'});
            $('.header-fixed').css({'height':'125px','margin-top':'-10px'});
            //ponistavanje stilova sa weba
                $(".js-submenu-category-item-first-level").unbind('mouseleave');                     
                $(".js-second-level").unbind('mouseleave');
                $(".js-category-menu").unbind('hover');
                $(window).unbind('scroll');
                  $(window).scroll(function () {
                      //console.log('123456');
                      if(!$('body').hasClass('one-page-checkout')){
                  if($(window).scrollTop() > 15 && !$('.header-user>div').children().hasClass('js-scroll-header'))  {
                     console.log('scrolllll');
                     
                    $('.header-fixed-wrap').css({'height':'55px','margin-top':'0'});
                     $('.header-fixed').css({'height':'55px','margin-top':'0'});
                     $('.search-form').css('display', 'none');
                     $('.header-user>div').prepend('<i class="thm-search js-scroll-header"></i>');
                      $('.sort-wrap').animate({top:'115px'});
                     $('.js-scroll-header').click(function() {
                     
                        console.log($('.search-form'));
                        if($('.search-form').css('display') === 'block'){ 
                            $('.search-form').slideUp();
                           $('.header-fixed-wrap').css({'height':'55px','margin-top':'0'});
                     $('.header-fixed').css({'height':'55px','margin-top':'0'});
                            }
                        else if ($('.search-form').css('display') === 'none') {
                            $('.search-form').slideDown();
                           
                             $('.header-fixed-wrap').animate({height:'125px','margin-top':'0'});
                            $('.header-fixed').animate({height:'125px','margin-top':'-10px'});
                           
                            
                        }
                     });
                 }
                 else if($(window).scrollTop()<1 && $('.header-user>div').children().hasClass('js-scroll-header') ){
                    $('.header-fixed-wrap').animate({height:'125px','margin-top':'0'});
                            $('.header-fixed').animate({height:'125px','margin-top':'-10px'});
                     $('.sort-wrap').animate({top:'184px'});
                     $('.search-form').css('display', 'block');
                     $('.header-user>div .thm-search').remove();
                 }
                      } 
             });
                  
            $('.category-menu i').removeAttr("style");
            $('.category-menu-wrap').removeAttr("style");
            $('.homepage .category-menu-wrap').removeAttr("style");
            $('.homepage .category-menu-wrap .category-menu-item0').removeAttr("style");
            $('.homepage .category-menu-item0').children().children('.first-level-link').removeAttr("style"); 
            $('.homepage .category-wrap ').unbind('mouseover');
            $('.homepage .category-wrap ').unbind('mouseleave');
            $('.js-second-level').removeClass('open-menu');
            $('.js-third-level-wrap').removeClass('open-menu');

            });


            $(".js-category-menu").click(function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();

                //console.log('otvaranje i zatvaranje menija na mobilnom');

                var $docEl = $('html, body'),
                    $wrap = $('.mob'),
                    scrollTop;

                $.lockBody = function() {
                    if(window.pageYOffset) {
                        scrollTop = window.pageYOffset;

                        $wrap.css({
                            top: - (scrollTop)
                        });
                    }

                    $docEl.css({
                        height: "100%",
                        overflow: "hidden"
                    });
                };

                $.unlockBody = function() {
                    $docEl.css({
                        height: "",
                        overflow: ""
                    });

                    $wrap.css({
                        top: ''
                    });

                    window.scrollTo(0, scrollTop);
                    window.setTimeout(function () {
                        scrollTop = null;
                    }, 0);
                };

                $('.js-header-links').css('display','none');

                $('.js-header-scroll').slideToggle('fast', function(){
                    if($(this).css('display')==='block'){
                        $.lockBody();
                        $('header').addClass('open-menu');
                        $('html').css('overflow','hidden');
                        $('body').on('touchmove',function(e){
                            if(!$('.scroll-category').has($(e.target)).length)
                                e.preventDefault();
                        });
                    }
                    else if($(this).css('display')==='none'){
                        $('html').css('overflow','scroll');
                        $('body').unbind('touchmove');
                        $('header').removeClass('open-menu');
                        $.unlockBody();
                    }
                });
                $(this).addClass('transparency');                                       
            });  
            $(".js-header-scroll .js-category-menu").click(function (e) {
                $(".js-category-menu.transparency").removeClass('transparency');
                $('.js-second-level').hide();
                $('.js-third-level-wrap').hide();
                $('.js-second-level').removeClass('open-menu');
                $('.js-third-level-wrap').removeClass('open-menu');
            });
            $(".js-submenu-category-item-first-level").click(function (e) {
                if($(this).children('ul').length > 0){
                    e.preventDefault();
                }
                e.stopPropagation();
                console.log('otvaranje i zatvaranje drugog nivo menija na mobilnom');

                $(this).children('.js-second-level').addClass('open-menu');
            });
            $(".close-menu").click(function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                $('.js-second-level').removeClass('open-menu');
                $('.js-third-level-wrap').removeClass('open-menu');
            });
            
            $(".js-second-level-category").unbind('click');
            $(".js-second-level-category").click(function (e) {                      
                if($(this).next('span').children('li') && $(this).next('span').children('li').length){
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    console.log('otvaranje i zatvaranje treceg nivo menija na mobilnom');
                    if($(this).next('span').hasClass('open-menu')){
                        $(this).next('span').removeClass('open-menu');
                    }else{
                        $('.js-third-level-wrap').removeClass('open-menu');
                        $(this).next('span').addClass('open-menu');
                    }
                } 
                else{
                    $(this).unbind(e);
                    $(".category-menu-item0").slideUp();
                    $(".category-menu-item1").slideUp();
                    $(".third-level-wrap").slideUp();     
                    $(".js-header-scroll").hide();
                }
            });
         
        }
        
        function categoryWeb() {
            $(window).unbind('scroll');
            $(window).unbind('click');
            $('html').attr("style", "");
            $('body').attr("style", "");
            $('.search-form').css('display', 'block');
            $('.header-fixed-wrap').css('height', '55px');
            $('.header-fixed').css({'height':'55px','margin-top':'0'});
            $('.sort-wrap').animate({top:'0'});
            $('header').removeClass('open-menu');
              $(function(){
            $(".js-category-menu-wrap").menuAim({
		activate: function(a){
                     var browserWidth = window.innerWidth;
                     if(browserWidth > 1024){
                         var idx = $(a).index();
                        // console.log('activate' +idx);
			$('.js-second-level').eq(idx).show();
                     }			
		},  // fired on row activation
		deactivate: function(a){
			var idx = $(a).index();
                        // console.log('dectivate' +idx);
			$('.js-second-level').eq(idx).hide();
			
		} ,
               
                exitMenu: function() {
                       $('.js-second-level').hide(); 
                       
    }
                
            // fired on row deactivation
	});
    });
        
            //console.log('function categoryWeb');
            scroledPage();
            $(window).scroll(function () {
                //console.log('scroll na webu');
                scroledPage();
            });      
            
            //ponistavanje klika sa mobilnog
            $(".js-category-menu").unbind('click');
            $(".js-category-menu.transparency").removeClass('transparency');
        }
                
        function scroledPage(){
            // console.log('provera skrola i adekvatno stilizovanje menija na webu')
            var browserWidth = window.innerWidth;
            var hideMenu1= $('#home-banner-web-js').height() + 26;
            // console.log(hideMenu1);
         
            var hideMenu =  hideMenu1 + 30;
            // console.log(hideMenu);
            if(!$('body').hasClass('homepage')){
                hideMenu=55;
            }
           
            if(browserWidth>1024){
                $(".js-category-menu").hover(function(){
                    $('.category-menu-wrap').css({'visibility':'visible', 'opacity':'1'});
                }, function(){
                    $('.category-menu-wrap').css({'visibility':'hidden', 'opacity':'0'});
                });
                $(".js-submenu-category-item-first-level").mouseover(function(){
                    $('.category-menu-wrap').css({'visibility':'visible', 'opacity':'1'});
                });
                $(".js-submenu-category-item-first-level").mouseleave(function(){
                    $('.category-menu-wrap').css({'visibility':'hidden', 'opacity':'0'});
                });
                $(".js-second-level").mouseleave(function(){
                    $('.category-menu-wrap').css({'visibility':'hidden', 'opacity':'0'});
                });
                
                if($('body').hasClass('homepage')){
                      
                    if($(window).scrollTop() > hideMenu){
                        $('.homepage .category-menu i').css({'position': 'fixed', 'z-index':' 11', 'color':'#ffcb05', 'top':'20px', 'padding-bottom':'18px', 'padding-right':'10px'});
                        $('.homepage .category-menu-wrap').css({'position': 'fixed', 'top':'55px'});
                        $('.homepage .category-menu-wrap').removeClass('show-menu');

                        var elem = $(".homepage .category-menu-wrap");
                        elem[0].style.setProperty('visibility', 'hidden', 'important');
                        elem[0].style.setProperty('opacity', '0');

                    }else{
                      
                        $(".js-submenu-category-item-first-level").unbind('mouseleave');                       
                        $(".js-second-level").unbind('mouseleave');
                        $(".js-category-menu").unbind('hover');
                        
                        $('.homepage .category-menu-wrap ').addClass('show-menu');
                        $('.homepage .js-header-scroll').show();
                        $('.homepage .category-menu i').css({'position': 'relative', 'z-index': 11,'color':'black', 'top':'0', 'padding-bottom':'0', 'padding-right':'0'});
                        $('.homepage .category-menu-wrap').css({'position': 'relative', 'top': '0'})
                        $('.homepage .category-menu-wrap').css({'visibility':'visible', 'opacity':'1'});
                    }
                }else{
                    var elem = $(".category-menu-wrap");
                        elem[0].style.setProperty('visibility', 'hidden', 'important');
                        elem[0].style.setProperty('opacity', '0');
                    if ($(window).scrollTop() > hideMenu) {
                        $('.js-header-scroll').show();
                        $('.category-menu i').css({'position': 'fixed', 'z-index':' 11', 'color':'#ffcb05', 'top':'20px','padding-bottom':'18px', 'padding-right':'23px','padding-left':'15px'});
                        $('.category-menu-wrap').css({'position': 'fixed', 'top':'50px','width':'100%', 'max-width':'1594px'});

                    }else{                    
                        $('.category-menu i').css({'position': 'relative', 'z-index': 11,'color':'black', 'top':'0', 'padding-bottom':'0', 'padding-right':'0','padding-left':'0'});
                        $('.category-menu-wrap').css({'position': 'relative', 'top': '0'});                             
                    }
                }
            }
    
           $('.js-third-level-wrap').removeAttr("style");
        } 
           
        $(document).ready(function () {
            //categoryMenu pokrece skripte za prikzaivanje menija
            categoryMenu();  
        });
        
       $(window).resize(function () { 
          
            // slucaj gde treba da se promeni izgled menija na resize
            var browserWidth = window.innerWidth;   
            
            //provera da li se preslo sa mobilnog na web ili obrnuto i pozivanje adekvatnog stila menija
            if((browserWidth > 1024 && $('body').hasClass('mob')) || (browserWidth < 1025 && $('body').hasClass('web'))){
               //console.log('prelaz sa mobilnog na web i obrnuto');
               categoryMenu();                  
               $(window).scrollTop(0);
            }
               if(browserWidth>1024){
                $("body").addClass('web');
                $("body").removeClass('mob');  
            }else if(browserWidth<1025){
                $("body").addClass('mob');
                $("body").removeClass('web');  
            }  
                                             
        });

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function () {      
            //skripta za input polja
             $(".js-input-field").each(function () {
                var inputHasValue = $(this).val().length > 0;
               
                if (inputHasValue) {
                    $(this).addClass('smallerLabel');
                }
            });

            $(".js-input-field").blur(function () {
                var inputHasValue = $(this).val().length > 0;                
                if (inputHasValue) {
                    $(this).addClass('smallerLabel');
                } else {
                    $(this).removeClass('smallerLabel');
                }
            });

            $('.js-input-field').bind('input', function () {
                $(this).addClass('smallerLabel');
            });

            setTimeout(function (e) {
                $(".js-input-field:-webkit-autofill").addClass('smallerLabel');
                $(".js-input-field:-moz-autofill").addClass('smallerLabel');
            }, 500);
  $('.js-input-field[type=text]').bind("change keyup",function(){

   $('.js-input-field[type=text]').each(function(){
    if ($(this).val().length > 0){
      $(this).addClass("smallerLabel");
    }
});
});
        });

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var rotate_product_id, rotate_product_timeout_id, rotate_product_first_start;
    // menjanje slike na hover proizvoda
    $(function () {
        rotate_product_first_start = true;

        $('.product-wrap-grid').on('mouseover', function () {
            rotateProductImage('grid/list', $(this).children('.product-img-wrap-grid').children('img'));
        }).on('mouseleave', function () {
            clearRotatedProductImage();
        });

        $('.product-square-item').on('mouseover', '.product-item-image img', function () {
            rotateProductImage('grid/list', this);
        }).on('mouseleave', '.product-item-image .link', function () {
            clearRotatedProductImage();
        });

        $('.product_list_cell').on('mouseover', '.itemListElement-img img', function () {
            rotateProductImage('grid/list', this);
        }).on('mouseleave', '.itemListElement-img a', function () {
            clearRotatedProductImage();
        });

        $('.promo-panel-item').on('mouseover', '.panel-image img', function () {
            rotateProductImage('slider', this);
        }).on('mouseleave', '.panel-image .link', function () {
            clearRotatedProductImage();
        });
    });

    function rotateProductImage(location, element) {
        var hideSelector = $(element);
        var imageInfo = $(element).data() && $(element).data().imageInfo ? $(element).data().imageInfo : '';
        var split = $(element).attr('id') ? $(element).attr('id').split('_') : [];
        var showSelector = '';
        var duration = 2000;

        if (location == 'slider') {
            rotate_product_id = split[2] + '_' + split[3];
        } else if (location = 'grid/list') {
            rotate_product_id = split[2];
        }

        if (imageInfo == 'main-image') {
            showSelector = $('#additional_pic_' + rotate_product_id);
        } else {
            showSelector = $('#prod_pic_' + rotate_product_id);
        }

        if (rotate_product_first_start == true) {
            duration = 1000;
            rotate_product_first_start = false;
        }

        if (showSelector.length) {
            rotate_product_timeout_id = setTimeout(function () {
                hideSelector.hide();
                showSelector.show();
            }, duration);
        }
    }

    function clearRotatedProductImage() {
        clearTimeout(rotate_product_timeout_id);
        $('#prod_pic_' + rotate_product_id).show();
        $('#additional_pic_' + rotate_product_id).hide();
        rotate_product_first_start = true;
    }
  </script>
  <script>
   // EC-490 - Implementation of custom popup system
        $(function () {
            $(".js-custom-popover").popover({
                trigger: "manual",
                html: true,
                placement: $(this).data("placement")
            }).on("mouseenter", function () {
                var _this = this;

                $(this).popover("show");

                $(".popover").on("mouseleave", function () {
                    $(_this).popover('hide');
                });
            }).on("mouseleave", function () {
                var _this = this;

                setTimeout(function () {
                    if (!$(".popover:hover").length) {
                        $(_this).popover("hide");
                    }
                }, 100);
            });
            $('.js-custom-popover').popover({html: true});
        });
  </script>
  <script>
   function lista_zelja_on_click(product_id)
        {
            $.ajax({url: $('[data-wish-list-id="' + product_id + '"]').attr("href"),
                type: 'post',
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (data) {
                    if (typeof data['url'] != "undefined" && data['url'] != '' && data['url'] != null)
                    {
                        window.location.href = data['url'];
                    }
                    else if (data['result'] == 'insert')
                    {
                        var link_text = $('[data-wish-list-id="' + product_id + '"]').attr("href");
                        link_text = link_text.replace("insert_pd", "del_wish_item");
                        $('[data-wish-list-id="' + product_id + '"]').has('.thm-heart-outline-round').html('<i class="thm-heart-fill-round"></i>');
                        $('[data-wish-list-id="' + product_id + '"]').prop("href", link_text);
                        insertWishItemIntoHeader(data);
                    }
                    else if (data['result'] == 'delete')
                    {
                        var link_text = $('[data-wish-list-id="' + product_id + '"]').attr("href");
                        link_text = link_text.replace("del_wish_item", "insert_pd");
                        $('[data-wish-list-id="' + product_id + '"]').has('.thm-heart-fill-round').html('<i class="thm-heart-outline-round"></i>');
                        $('[data-wish-list-id="' + product_id + '"]').prop("href", link_text);
                        $('[data-header-wish-list-id="' + product_id + '"]').remove();
                        if (!data['wish_list']) {
                            $('.js-wish-list-content').remove();
                        }
                        insertWishItemIntoHeader(data);
                    }
                },
                error: function (data) {
                    console.log(data);
                }
            });
            return false;
        }
        function insertWishItemIntoHeader(data)
        {
            $('.header-basket-content-js').removeClass('js-shown-basket');
            
            var products = data['wish_list'];
            var is_shown = $('.js-wish-list-content').hasClass('js-shown-wish');
            var shown_class = '';
            if (is_shown) {
                shown_class = 'js-shown-wish';
            }
            var content_html = '<div class="wish-list-content js-wish-list-content '+ shown_class +'">';
            for (var item in products) {
                var old_price = 0;
                var savings = 0;
                var price = 0;
                price = parseInt(products[item].cena_niza_redovna).toLocaleString(
                        'de-DE',
                        {
                            style: 'currency',
                            currency: CURRENCY,
                            minimumFractionDigits: 0
                        }
                );
                if (products[item].price > products[item].cena_niza_redovna) {
                    savings = 'usteda ' + parseInt(products[item].price - products[item].cena_niza_redovna).toLocaleString(
                            'de-DE',
                            {
                                style: 'currency',
                                currency: CURRENCY,
                                minimumFractionDigits: 0
                            }
                    );
                    old_price = parseInt(products[item].price).toLocaleString(
                            'de-DE',
                            {
                                style: 'currency',
                                currency: CURRENCY,
                                minimumFractionDigits: 0
                            }
                    );
                }
                if(old_price == 0){
                    old_price = '';
                }
                if(savings == 0){
                    savings = '';
                }
                content_html += '<div class="header-basket-product" data-header-wish-list-id="' + products[item].product_id + '">\n\
                                                <a class="product-link" href="' + HOME + products[item].sef_name.html + '"></a>\n\
                                                <div class="basket-image-wrapper">\n\
                                                    <img src="' + HOME + 'UserFiles/products/small/' + products[item].image + '"/>\n\
                                                    <span class="vertical"></span>\n\
                                                </div>\n\
                                                <div class="header-basket-product-title">\n\
                                                    ' + products[item].name + '\n\
                                                </div>\n\
                                                <div class="product-price-header">\n\
                                                    <div class="old-price">\n\
                                                            ' + old_price + '\n\
                                                    </div>\n\
                                                    <div class="savings">\n\
                                                            ' + savings + '\n\
                                                    </div>\n\
                                                    <div class="price">\n\
                                                        ' + price + '\n\
                                                    </div>\n\
                                                </div>\n\
                                                <a class="delete-product js-wish-list" onclick="return lista_zelja_on_click(' + products[item].product_id + ');" target="_blank" href="' + HOME + 'index.php?mod=lists&op=wish_list&product_id=' + products[item].product_id + '&del_wish_item=1&json=1&wish_list_vote=1 rel="nofollow">\n\
                                                    <i class="thm-dismiss"></i>\n\
                                                </a>\n\
                                            </div>';
            }
            if (data['user'] == 'not_logged') {
                content_html += '<div class="total-basket-value-wrap"><div class="basket-header-button"><a class="" href="' + HOME + '/index.php?mod=customers&op=register">Sačuvaj listu </a></div></div>';
            } else {
                content_html += '<div class="total-basket-value-wrap"><div class="basket-header-button"><a class="" href="' + HOME + '/index.php?mod=lists&op=wish_list">Sačuvaj listu </a></div></div>';
            }
            $('.js-wish-list-content').remove();
            $('.js-wish-list-wrap').append(content_html);
            
            if (!is_shown) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    $('.js-wish-list-content').addClass('js-shown-wish');
                    var wishContent = $('.js-wish-list-content');
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        wishContent.removeClass('js-shown-wish');
                    }, 3000);
                }, 10);
            } else {
                var wishContent = $('.js-wish-list-content');
                setTimeout(function () {
                    wishContent.removeClass('js-shown-wish');
                }, 3000);
            }
        }
  </script>

  <script src="https://www.tehnomanija.rs/common/javascript/countdown/jquery.countdown.js">
  </script>
  <script>
   $(document).ready(function () {
        $('[data-countdown]').each(function () {
            var $this = $(this), finalDate = $(this).data('countdown');
            var fd = finalDate.split(/[- :]/);
            var endDate = new Date(fd[0], fd[1] - 1, fd[2], fd[3], fd[4], fd[5]);

            if (finalDate != '-' && finalDate != '') {
                $(this).css('visibility', 'visible');
                $this.countdown(endDate, function (event) {
                    var date = parseInt(event.strftime('%D'), 10);
                    if (date > 1) {
                        $(this).html(event.strftime('<div><i class="thm-timer"></i>' + date + '<span>d</span></div><div> %H<span>h</span></div><div> %M<span>m</span></div><div> %S<span>s</span><div>'));
                    }
                }).on('finish.countdown', function () {
                    $(this).delay(5000).hide(1);//css('visibility', 'hidden');
                });
            }
        });

    });
  </script>

  <script>
   $('.fnc-header-login .login-link').click(function (event) {
            event.stopPropagation();
        });
        $('.fnc-header-login').click(function (event) { // Add event for logging user

            $('.js-errorbox').hide(); // Hide all old messages
            event.preventDefault();
            var email = $('.js-header-email').val();
            var password = $('.js-header-password').val().trim();

            if (password == '') {
                $('.js-password-is-mandatory').show(); // Show message password is mandatory
            } else {
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: "//www.tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=customers&op=ajax_one_page_checkout&act=login",
                    dataType: "json",
                    data: {
                        'email': email,
                        'password': password
                    },
                    success: function(data) {
                        console.log(data);
                        var message;
                        if (data.status == 'customer_logged') {
                            user_is_logged = true;
                            setHeaderUser(data);
                            location.reload();
                            // window.location.href = data.redirect;
                        } else if (data.status == 'wrong_password') {
                            message = 'Korisničko ime ili password nisu ispravni';
                            $('[data-error-message="true"]').html(message).show()
                        } else if (data.status == 'customer_not_found') {
                            message = 'Korisničko ime ili password nisu ispravni';
                            $('[data-error-message="true"]').html(message).show()
                        }
                    },
                    error:function(jqXHR, exception){
                        console.info('error while logging in:', jqXHR, exception);
                    }
                });
            }
        });
        function setHeaderUser(data){
            var headerHtml = '<div class="user-wraper"><div><i class="thm-user-outline"></i>\n\
                                    <span class="user-name">'+ data.customer.first_name +'</span></div>\n\
                                    <div class="dropdown-login logged-in">\n\
                                        <a href="https://tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=customers&amp;op=my_account">Moj nalog</a>\n\
                                        <a href="https://tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=customers&amp;op=my_orders">Moje narudžbenice</a>\n\
                                        <a href="https://tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=lists&amp;op=wish_list">Lista želja</a>\n\
                                        <a href="https://tehnomanija.rs/index.php?mod=customers&amp;op=logout">Odjava</a>\n\
                                    </div>\n\
                                </div>';
            $('.user-wraper').replaceWith(headerHtml);              
        }

  <script>
   isLocalStorageNameSupported = function() {
    var testKey = 'test', storage = window.sessionStorage;
    try {
        storage.setItem(testKey, '1');
        storage.removeItem(testKey);
        return true;
    } catch (error) {
        return false;
    }
}
  </script>
  <script>
   $(document).ready(function () {
                if(isLocalStorageNameSupported()){
               if(sessionStorage.firstTimeVisited != "true" && sessionStorage.firstTimeVisited != "close"){ 
                   sessionStorage.firstTimeVisited=true;
                  
                  $('.app-link').css({'visibility': 'visible', 'opacity':'1', 'height':'0', 'overflow':'visible'});
                  setTimeout(function(){
                             $('.app-link p').trigger("click");
                        }, 500);
                  
              }else if(sessionStorage.firstTimeVisited == "close"){
                  $('.app-link').hide();
                
              }else if(sessionStorage.firstTimeVisited == "true"){
                  
                  $('.app-link').css({'visibility': 'visible', 'opacity':'1', 'height':'0', 'overflow':'visible'});
              }
              
                (function () {

       var BrowserDetect = {
            init: function () {
                this.version = this.searchVersion(navigator.userAgent)
                    || this.searchVersion(navigator.appVersion)
                    || "an unknown version";
                this.OS = this.searchString(this.dataOS) || "an unknown OS";
            },
            searchString: function (data) {
                for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
                    var dataString = data[i].string;
                    var dataProp = data[i].prop;
                    this.versionSearchString = data[i].versionSearch || data[i].identity;
                    if (dataString) {
                        if (dataString.indexOf(data[i].subString) != -1)
                            return data[i].identity;
                    }
                    else if (dataProp)
                        return data[i].identity;
                }
            },
            searchVersion: function (dataString) {
                var index = dataString.indexOf(this.versionSearchString);
                if (index == -1) return;
                return parseFloat(dataString.substring(index + this.versionSearchString.length + 1));
            },          
            dataOS: [
                {
                    string: navigator.platform,
                    subString: "Win",
                    identity: "Windows"
                },
                {
                    string: navigator.platform,
                    subString: "Mac",
                    identity: "Mac"
                },
                {
                    string: navigator.platform,
                    subString: "iPad",
                    identity: "iPad"
                },
                {
                    string: navigator.userAgent,
                    subString: "iPhone",
                    identity: "iPhone/iPod"
                },
                {
                    string: navigator.userAgent,
                    subString: "Android",
                    identity: "Android"
                },
                  {
                    string: navigator.platform,
                    subString: "Linux",
                    identity: "Linux"
                }
            ]

        };

       BrowserDetect.init();

        window.$.client = {os: BrowserDetect.OS};


    })();
               if($.client.os == 'iPhone/iPod' || $.client.os == 'iPad' ){
                    $('.app-link').css({'visibility': 'visible', 'opacity':'1', 'height':'0', 'overflow':'visible'});
                    $('#app-go a').attr("href", "https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/tehnomanija/id889607803?mt=8#");
                }
                else if($.client.os == 'Windows' || $.client.os == 'Linux' || $.client.os == 'Mac' ){
                    sessionStorage.firstTimeVisited="close";
                    $('.app-link').hide();
                  
                }
                else{
                    $('.app-link').css({'visibility': 'visible', 'opacity':'1', 'height':'0', 'overflow':'visible'});
                    $('#app-go a').attr("href", "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=rs.netlink.android&hl=rs");
                }
             
          
                
              
                    $('#app-popup-close, #app-go').click(function(){
               
                        $('.app-popup').addClass('closed-app-popup').css('visibility','hidden');

                        setTimeout(function(){

                    });
                    $('.app-link p').click(function(){
                        $('.app-popup').removeClass('closed-app-popup').css('visibility','visible');
                        $('.app-popup-inner').removeClass('closed-app-inner-popup');

                     $('#app-popup-close').click(function(e){

  <style>
   /* just to be sure these are full screen*/


            #gameCanvas {

                pointer-events: none !important;
                position: absolute;
                top: 0;
                left: 0;
                bottom: 0;
                display:block;

            }
  </style>
  <canvas id="gameCanvas" style="z-index: 999999;">
  </canvas>
  <script>
   $(document).ready(function () {
                /*var stickerbottom = $('#home-banner-web-js').height() - 13;
              $('.sticker-wrap').css('top',500);*/
                var dpi = window.devicePixelRatio;
                var bannerPocetna = $('#home-banner-web-js'),
                    offsetBannerPocetna = bannerPocetna.offset(),
                    canvasGameElement = $('#gameCanvas'), logoElement = $('.logo-wrap');

                canvasGameElement.css('top', 0);
                canvasGameElement.css('left', offsetBannerPocetna.left);

                var canvas,
                    ctx,
                    cx = 100,
                    cy = 100,
                    vx = 2,
                    vy = 5,
                    radius = 25,//radius of image
                    gravity = 0.95,
                    damping = 0.75,//number for ball jumps
                    traction = 0.8,
                    image,
                    flag,
                    imageWidth = 50,
                    imageHeight = 50,
                    paused = false,
                    animation = 0,
                    animationTimeout = 200,
                    loopimg = 0,
                    debug = false;


                var ball = function () {
                    // var startAngle = 0, endAngle = 2 * Math.PI, counterClockwise = false;
                    if (debug) {
                        console.log('ball::');
                    }

                    canvas = document.getElementById("gameCanvas");
                    if (!canvas) {
                        return;
                    }
                    ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

                    // canvas.width = 1920;
                    canvas.width = $(bannerPocetna).width();
                    canvas.height = $(bannerPocetna).height() + 85;
                    // canvas.height = 600;


                    if (debug) {
                        console.log('canvas.width:', canvas.width);
                        console.log('canvas.height:', canvas.height);
                    }
                    image = new Image();
                    image.src = 'https://www.tehnomanija.rs/themes/smarty_new_design/assets/images/FWC2018-100x100.png';

                    flag = new Image();
                    flag.src = 'https://www.tehnomanija.rs/themes/smarty_new_design/assets/images/flag.png';


                    if (cx + radius >= canvas.width) {
                        vx = -vx * damping;
                        cx = canvas.width - radius;
                    } else if (cx - radius <= 0) {
                        vx = -vx * damping;
                        cx = radius;
                    }
                    if (cy + radius >= canvas.height) {
                        vy = -vy * damping;
                        cy = canvas.height - radius;
                        // traction here
                        vx *= traction;
                    } else if (cy - radius <= 0) {
                        vy = -vy * damping;
                        cy = radius;
                    }


                    if (!paused && animation < animationTimeout) {
                        animation = requestAnimationFrame(ball);
                    }
                    if (animation >= animationTimeout) {

                        requestAnimationFrame(draw);


                        $('#gameCanvas').delay(1800).fadeOut('normal', function () {
                            $(this).remove();
                        })


                    }

                    vy += gravity;

                    cx -= vx;
                    cy += vy;

                    ctx.beginPath();

                    ctx.drawImage(image, cx - radius, cy - radius - 5, imageWidth, imageHeight);

                    // ctx.arc(cx, cy, radius, startAngle, endAngle, counterClockwise);


                    if (debug) {
                        console.log('end ball::');
                    }

                };

                function fix_dpi() {
                    //get CSS height
                    //the + prefix casts it to an integer
                    //the slice method gets rid of "px"

                    var style_height = +getComputedStyle(canvas).getPropertyValue("height").slice(0, -2);

                    //get CSS width
                    var style_width = +getComputedStyle(canvas).getPropertyValue("width").slice(0, -2);

                    //scale the canvas

                    canvas.setAttribute('height', style_height * dpi);
                    canvas.setAttribute('width', style_width * dpi);
                }

                function draw() {

                    canvas = document.getElementById("gameCanvas");

                    if (!canvas) {
                        return;
                    }


                    ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

                    flag = new Image();
                    flag.src = 'https://www.tehnomanija.rs/themes/smarty_new_design/assets/images/flag.png';

                    canvas.width = $(bannerPocetna).width();
                    canvas.height = $(bannerPocetna).height() + 85;

                    ctx.beginPath();
                    ctx.drawImage(image, cx - radius, cy - radius - 5, 50, 50);

                    ctx.fillStyle = 'hsl(0, 100%, 0%)';
                    ctx.font = 'normal  26px "Roboto"';

                    var text = "Navijamo zajedno za Srbiju";

                    ctx.fillText(text.substr(0, loopimg), cx + 30, cy + 5);

                    loopimg++;

                    var len = text.length + 1;

                    if (loopimg < len) {
                        requestAnimationFrame(draw);
                    }

                    // if (loopimg == len) {
                    ctx.drawImage(flag, cx + 355, cy - 12, 30, 20);
                    // }

                }

                var handleMouseDown = function (e, canvas) {
                    if (debug) {
                        console.log('handleMouseDown');
                        console.log('E:', e);
                        console.log('e.pageX:', e.pageX);
                        console.log('e.pageY:', e.pageY);
                        console.log('canvas.offsetLeft:', canvas.offsetLeft);
                        console.log('canvas.offsetTop:', canvas.offsetTop);
                    }
                    cx = e.pageX - canvas.offsetLeft;
                    cy = e.pageY - canvas.offsetTop;
                    if (debug) {
                        console.log('cx:', cx, 'cy: ', cy);
                    }
                    vx = vy = 0;
                    paused = true;
                };

                var handleMouseUp = function (e, canvas) {
                    if (debug) {
                        console.log('handleMouseUp');
                        console.log('E:', e);
                        console.log('e.pageX:', e.pageX);
                        console.log('e.pageY:', e.pageY);
                        console.log('canvas.offsetLeft:', canvas.offsetLeft);
                        console.log('canvas.offsetTop:', canvas.offsetTop);
                    }
                    // e.pageX = 0, e.pageY = 0;
                    vx = e.pageX - canvas.offsetLeft - cx;
                    vy = e.pageY - canvas.offsetTop - cy;
                    if (debug) {
                        console.log('vx:', vx, 'vy: ', vy);
                    }
                    paused = false;
                    ball();
                };

//get DPI

// fancy/irrelevant mouse grab'n'throw stuff below
//             document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleMouseDown);
//             document.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);

                // var off = $("*", document.body).offset();
                var logoOffset = logoElement.offset().left + 155;

                var el = {
                    pageX: logoOffset,
                    pageY: 20
                };

                var elcanv = {
                    offsetLeft: 0,
                    offsetTop: 0
                };

                handleMouseDown(el, elcanv);

                var el2 = {
                    pageX: logoOffset - 4,
                    pageY: 20
                };

                handleMouseUp(el2, elcanv);

            });
  </script>
 </body>
